     <p>
      This is a
      <b>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_social_nudity_places" title="List of social nudity places">
        list of social nudity places
       </a>
       in Europe
      </b>
      for recreation. It includes free beaches (or clothing-optional beaches or
      <a href="/wiki/Nude_beach" title="Nude beach">
       nude beaches
      </a>
      ) and some resorts.
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Belgium">
       Belgium
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Belgium">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Topfree sunbathing is tolerated on all beaches.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2014)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Bredene" title="Bredene">
        Bredene
       </a>
       is the only official nude beach in Belgium.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.camping-grensland.be" rel="nofollow">
        Naturistencamping Grensland
       </a>
       is a small nude camping near to
       <a href="/wiki/Antwerp" title="Antwerp">
        Antwerp
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Croatia">
       Croatia
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Croatia">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lokrum_nude_beach.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="357" data-file-width="300" height="262" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f4/Lokrum_nude_beach.jpg/220px-Lokrum_nude_beach.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f4/Lokrum_nude_beach.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/f/f4/Lokrum_nude_beach.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Lokrum_nude_beach.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Lokrum
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Croatia has a well developed naturist culture with camp sites and hotels specifically catering for naturists. Naturism has been big in Croatia ever since
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_Edward_VIII" title="King Edward VIII">
       King Edward VIII
      </a>
      and his then mistress,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wallace_Simpson" title="Wallace Simpson">
       Wallace Simpson
      </a>
      , were allowed to swim nude at one of Rab's beaches in 1936.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-coom_Kaya_1-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-coom_Kaya-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-web._Beac_2-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-web._Beac-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bradbury_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Bradbury-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Istria_peninsula">
       Istria peninsula
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Dalmatia">
       Dalmatia
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Dalmatia">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      In
      <a href="/wiki/Dalmatia" title="Dalmatia">
       Dalmatia
      </a>
      gulf the following nude beaches and resorts can be found:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Kasuni_(Split)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Kasuni (Split) (page does not exist)">
        Kasuni
       </a>
       beach,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Split_(city)" title="Split (city)">
        Split
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nugal" title="Nugal">
        Nugal
       </a>
       beach, between
       <a href="/wiki/Makarska" title="Makarska">
        Makarska
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tucepi" title="Tucepi">
        Tucepi
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Sveti_Petar_(Makarska,_Croatia)" title="Sveti Petar (Makarska, Croatia)">
        Sv. Petar
       </a>
       beach, central
       <a href="/wiki/Makarska" title="Makarska">
        Makarska
       </a>
       town.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Lokrum" title="Lokrum">
        Lokrum
       </a>
       island (beach),
       <a href="/wiki/Dubrovnik" title="Dubrovnik">
        Dubrovnik
       </a>
       .
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Czech_Republic">
       Czech Republic
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Czech Republic">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Topfree is tolerated on all places.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2012)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
      Public nudity is not illegal in the Czech Republic, but it may be regulated by local authorities.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2014)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       There are about one hundred officially recognized naturist localities; see
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.naturista.cz/lokality/ftexta1.htm" rel="nofollow">
        list of places
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Denmark">
       Denmark
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Denmark">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Since 1976 it is permissible to be nude at any beach in Denmark, except for two.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2015)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
      There are more than 7,000 kilometres (4,300mi) of coastline to choose from. A large number of clothing-optional beaches exist throughout the country.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
       <a href="#cite_note-13">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        13
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The beach at the village of Husby in the
      <a href="/wiki/Holstebro_Municipality" title="Holstebro Municipality">
       Holstebro Municipality
      </a>
      is being promoted as a
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FKK" title="FKK">
       FKK
      </a>
      beach.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tvmi_Hols_14-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-tvmi_Hols-14">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        14
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Estonia">
       Estonia
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Estonia">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Estonian naturist beaches are overseen by NGO Estnat (closed in 2012
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
       <a href="#cite_note-15">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        15
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      ). No tickets are necessary.
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Tallinn" title="Tallinn">
        Tallinn
       </a>
       , an unofficial, but tolerated naturist beach. Situated about 3km north-east of the ferry port, at the very northern end of textiler beach.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Tartu" title="Tartu">
        Tartu
       </a>
       unofficial naturist lawn beach is situated right next the city one in the end of Ranna tee (on the other side of
       <a href="/wiki/Emaj%C3%B5gi" title="Emajgi">
        Emajgi
       </a>
       river from
       <a href="/wiki/Supilinn" title="Supilinn">
        Supilinna
       </a>
       pond.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/P%C3%A4rnu" title="Prnu">
        Prnu
       </a>
       , also unofficial but tolerated woman's and men's beach between official beach and Prnu river.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Narva-J%C3%B5esuu" title="Narva-Jesuu">
        Narva-Jesuu
       </a>
       nude beach - the only official nude beach in Estonia.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       Located near
       <a href="/wiki/Narva-J%C3%B5esuu" title="Narva-Jesuu">
        Narva-Jesuu
       </a>
       town, 2km SW from the town border.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Finland">
       Finland
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Finland">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Helsinki" title="Helsinki">
        Helsinki
       </a>
       :
       <ul>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Pihlajasaari" title="Pihlajasaari">
          Pihlajasaari
         </a>
         : Has a unisex nudist beach, consisting almost entirely of rocky
         <a href="/wiki/Cliff" title="Cliff">
          cliffs
         </a>
         , with no
         <a href="/wiki/Sand" title="Sand">
          sand
         </a>
         . Not very suitable for swimming.
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Seurasaari" title="Seurasaari">
          Seurasaari
         </a>
         : Separate nudist beaches for men and women. No unisex nudist area.
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Yrj%C3%B6nkatu_Swimming_Hall" title="Yrjnkatu Swimming Hall">
          Yrjnkatu Swimming Hall
         </a>
         : a swimming hall in a historic architecture. Gender separated by day of week.
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Pori" title="Pori">
        Pori
       </a>
       :
       <ul>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Yyteri" title="Yyteri">
          Yyteri
         </a>
         : A very small part of the main Yyteri beach is designated as a unisex nudist beach. A flat beach covered in sand and much more suitable for swimming than Pihlajasaari.
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="France">
       France
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: France">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">
      Main article:
      <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_French_nudist_beaches&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="List of French nudist beaches (page does not exist)">
       List of French nudist beaches
      </a>
     </div>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Port_Leucate_(Aude),_Oasis,_plage_naturiste.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="2592" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Port_Leucate_%28Aude%29%2C_Oasis%2C_plage_naturiste.jpg/220px-Port_Leucate_%28Aude%29%2C_Oasis%2C_plage_naturiste.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Port_Leucate_%28Aude%29%2C_Oasis%2C_plage_naturiste.jpg/330px-Port_Leucate_%28Aude%29%2C_Oasis%2C_plage_naturiste.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Port_Leucate_%28Aude%29%2C_Oasis%2C_plage_naturiste.jpg/440px-Port_Leucate_%28Aude%29%2C_Oasis%2C_plage_naturiste.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Port_Leucate_(Aude),_Oasis,_plage_naturiste.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Naturist beach at Port Leucate (Aude), France, which illustrates the mixed clothing habits on leading French beaches
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <ul>
      <li>
       There are many naturist resorts on the Atlantic coast, for example
       <a href="/wiki/CHM_Montalivet" title="CHM Montalivet">
        CHM Montalivet
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Euronat_(naturist_resort)" title="Euronat (naturist resort)">
        Euronat
       </a>
       and La Jenny.
      </li>
      <li>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">
        Mediterranean
       </a>
       seaside town of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cap_d%27Agde,_France" title="Cap d'Agde, France">
        Cap d'Agde
       </a>
       has a large naturist village with sandy beach, several swimming pools, but also nude shopping.
      </li>
      <li>
       Leucate
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
        <a href="#cite_note-16">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         16
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Naturist Villages, and a 1,200 metres (1,300yd) long beach is one the best places on Mediterranean to practise naturism
      </li>
      <li>
       Aphrodite Village, Oasis Village are open 300 days per year.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2015)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/%C3%8Ele_du_Levant" title="le du Levant">
        le du Levant
       </a>
       , an island in the
       <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">
        Mediterranean Sea
       </a>
       has a nudist town, Hliopolis, and a nudist beach known as Plage des Grottes.
      </li>
      <li>
       Plage de Pampelonne in
       <a href="/wiki/Ramatuelle" title="Ramatuelle">
        Ramatuelle
       </a>
       near
       <a href="/wiki/Saint-Tropez" title="Saint-Tropez">
        Saint-Tropez
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       Plage du Layet near
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Cavali%C3%A8re&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cavalire (page does not exist)">
        Cavalire
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       There are beaches on many rivers, some well known, some informal: Cze, Ardeche, Truyre
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Topfree_equality" title="Topfree equality">
        Topfreedom
       </a>
       is tolerated (and common) on almost all beaches
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>

       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_(2200637243).jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="703" data-file-width="1173" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_%282200637243%29.jpg/220px-FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_%282200637243%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_%282200637243%29.jpg/330px-FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_%282200637243%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_%282200637243%29.jpg/440px-FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_%282200637243%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:FKK-Gelande_Sudstrand_Strandimpressionen_(2200637243).jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Naturist beach in Germany.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Public nudity is not illegal in Germany but may be regulated by local authorities mostly because of safety and health issues, not morality. Apart from urban areas and public baths (which often offer nude swimming days), nude bathing is common in Germany: unofficial clothing optional areas exist at most lakes and rivers and other sites, such as abandoned sand and rock quarries. Many designated
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Freik%C3%B6rperkultur" title="Freikrperkultur">
        Freikrperkultur
       </a>
      </i>
      (FKK  Free Body Culture) areas exist at the seaside, at lakes and in baths, especially in the former
      <a href="/wiki/East_Germany" title="East Germany">
       East Germany
      </a>
      , where nudism remains more widespread than in the west. Many unregulated clothing optional (FKK) free beaches are available along the Nordsee and Baltic seashores,
      <a href="/wiki/R%C3%BCgen" title="Rgen">
       Rgen
      </a>
      and other islands. The attitude is: all beaches are nude beaches until somebody complains. Families especially like to spend their leisure time in naturist areas;
      <a href="/wiki/Sauna" title="Sauna">
       sauna
      </a>
      bathing is generally practiced in the nude.
     </p>
     <p>
      The list of social nudity places in Germany includes:
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-natu_Euro_380-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-natu_Euro-380">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        380
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       The Schnfeldwiese in the
       <a href="/wiki/Englischer_Garten" title="Englischer Garten">
        Englischer Garten
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Munich" title="Munich">
        Munich
       </a>
       as well as the southern part of Feldmochinger See, in the northwestern suburb, the peninsula in Lake
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Feringasee&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Feringasee (page does not exist)">
        Feringasee
       </a>
       in the northeast and the Flaucher at the river
       <a href="/wiki/Isar" title="Isar">
        Isar
       </a>
       south of the city center of Munich.
      </li>
      <li>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Tiergarten_(park)" title="Tiergarten (park)">
        Tiergarten
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">
        Berlin
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Wannsee" title="Wannsee">
        Wannsee
       </a>
       , Berlin
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Travem%C3%BCnde" title="Travemnde">
        Travemnde
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Sylt" title="Sylt">
        Sylt
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Gr%C3%B6mitz" title="Grmitz">
        Grmitz
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Borkum" title="Borkum">
        Borkum
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Baden-Baden" title="Baden-Baden">
        Baden-Baden
       </a>
       is a city located near the French border. This city has many natural mineral springs and numerous clothes free bath houses are located.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Greece">
       Greece
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Greece">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Crete_komos_beach.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1024" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Crete_komos_beach.jpg/220px-Crete_komos_beach.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Crete_komos_beach.jpg/330px-Crete_komos_beach.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Crete_komos_beach.jpg/440px-Crete_komos_beach.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Crete_komos_beach.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Komos Beach on the south coast of Crete, near Matala
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Naturism is practised widely in the Greek Islands although, strictly speaking, legal only in a relatively few designated locations but almost on all islands there are unofficial nudist beaches.
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Topfree" title="Topfree">
       Topfree
      </a>
      is tolerated on almost all beaches.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2009)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Crete">
       Crete
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Crete">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Beaches and resorts in
      <a href="/wiki/Crete" title="Crete">
       Crete
      </a>
      include:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Filaki beach the only official nudist beach near the Vritomartis naturist resort.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-381">
        <a href="#cite_note-381">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         381
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Glyka_Nera" title="Glyka Nera">
        Glyka Nera
       </a>
       near
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Loutro_(Chania),_Greece" title="Loutro (Chania), Greece">
        Loutro
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Diskos near Lentos.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Plakias" title="Plakias">
        Plakias
       </a>
       , the south-eastern part of the beach is used by naturists.
      </li>
      <li>
       North of
       <a href="/wiki/Matala,_Crete" title="Matala, Crete">
        Matala
       </a>
       there is a very long nude beach, the southern end of the beach is used by clothed people.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Sougia" title="Sougia">
        Sougia
       </a>
       , the eastern part of the beach if for nude bathing.
      </li>
     </ul>

        Sistiana
       </a>
       and
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Grignano&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Grignano (page does not exist)">
        Grignano
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Trieste" title="Trieste">
        Trieste
       </a>
        km. 143 state road 14, very difficult to reach.
      </li>
     </ul>

        </a>

          </span>

           </span>
          </span>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Sardinia">
       Sardinia
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Sardinia">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <p>
      Beaches in
      <a href="/wiki/Sardinia" title="Sardinia">
       Sardinia
      </a>
      are:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Hundreds of small, secluded beaches can occasionally become nudist corners. Traditional places are the beaches
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Cala_di_Volpe&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cala di Volpe (page does not exist)">
        Cala di Volpe
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Liscia_di_Vacca" title="Liscia di Vacca">
        Liscia di Vacca
       </a>
       , to the north of
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Pitrizza_Hotel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Pitrizza Hotel (page does not exist)">
        Pitrizza Hotel
       </a>
       and
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Piccolo_Pevero&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Piccolo Pevero (page does not exist)">
        Piccolo Pevero
       </a>
       beach, the far side to the right after the rocks.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Capo_Falcone&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Capo Falcone (page does not exist)">
        Capo Falcone
       </a>
       near
       <a href="/wiki/Stintino" title="Stintino">
        Stintino
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Marina di Arbus,
       <a href="/wiki/Costa_Verde_(Sardinia)" title="Costa Verde (Sardinia)">
        Costa Verde
       </a>
       . The rough west coast has lonely beaches and coves for sunbathing, where toplessness is usually possible (see picture below). The area is less developed for tourists, so you can enjoy nature.

        </a>
       </sup>
       Go to Macchiatonda beach, at the beach house you have to walk for 20 minutes east. A beautiful community of nudists on the weekends, quiet neighborhood, a beautiful beach, clear water . You can walk barefoot for miles. Located at
       <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion">
        <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;params=42_24_7_N_11_20_47_E_">

           <span class="latitude">
            42247N
           </span>
           <span class="longitude">
            112047E
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>

      </li>
      <li>
       Baia delle sirene nudist beach at
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Punta_S._Vigilio&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Punta S. Vigilio (page does not exist)">

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Latvia">
       Latvia
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Latvia">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Latvian naturist beaches are overseen by the "Latvian Naturist Association".
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Vec%C4%81%C4%B7i" title="Veci">
        Veci
       </a>
       official naturist beach. The biggest of Latvia's naturist beaches, situated a little way north of Veci village. To get there from Riga take the Riga-Saulkrasti railway line and get off at Veci or bus Nr24 or small bus Nr200&amp;224.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=In%C4%8Dupe&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Inupe (page does not exist)">
        Inupe
       </a>
       naturist beach. A medium-sized beach, situated near the
       <a href="/wiki/Saulkrasti" title="Saulkrasti">
        Saulkrasti
       </a>
       railway line on the southern bank of the Inupe river about 50km from Riga.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Lielupe" title="Lielupe">
        Lielupe
       </a>
       beach. A small, unofficial naturist beach, on the left bank of the Lielupe river delta.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ventspils" title="Ventspils">
        Ventspils
       </a>
       city has an official naturist beach.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Liep%C4%81ja" title="Liepja">
        Liepja
       </a>
       unofficial naturist beach. Also quite small, situated about 3km south of Liepaja.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Lithuania">
       Lithuania
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Lithuania">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Naturist beaches in Lithuania are overseen by local communities.
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Giruliai&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Giruliai (page does not exist)">
        Giruliai
       </a>
       naturist beach - A small official naturist beach in
       <a href="/wiki/Klaip%C4%97da" title="Klaipda">
        Klaipda
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Smiltyn%C4%97" title="Smiltyn">
        Smiltyn
       </a>
       naturist beach - A large official naturist beach in
       <a href="/wiki/Klaip%C4%97da" title="Klaipda">
        Klaipda
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Nida,_Lithuania" title="Nida, Lithuania">
        Nida
       </a>
       naturist beach - A very large, official naturist beach. Located on the north shore of the Curonian Spit, just a few kilometers east of the border of Russian
       <a href="/wiki/Kaliningrad" title="Kaliningrad">
        Kaliningrad
       </a>
       enclave.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0ventoji,_Lithuania" title="ventoji, Lithuania">
        ventoji
       </a>
       naturist beach - A small official naturist beach in
       <a href="/wiki/Palanga" title="Palanga">
        Palanga
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Nemirseta" title="Nemirseta">
        Nemirseta
       </a>
       beach - A small unofficial naturist beach in
       <a href="/wiki/Palanga" title="Palanga">
        Palanga
       </a>
       .
      </li>
     </ul>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Montenegro">
       Montenegro
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Montenegro">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ada_Bojana" title="Ada Bojana">
        Ada Bojana
       </a>
       , the biggest nudist beach in the country
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Jaz_Beach" title="Jaz Beach">
        Jaz
       </a>
       , the southernmost part of the beach used to be declared nudist but was made regular in 2007
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ratac" title="Ratac">
        Ratac
       </a>
       , is outside Bar in the direction of Budva, near
       <a href="/wiki/Sutomore" title="Sutomore">
        Sutomore
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       Njivice, a village on the south-western shore of the Bay of
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Hecrg_Novi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Hecrg Novi (page does not exist)">
        Hecrg Novi
       </a>
       (Boka Kotorska bay) the nudist beach is located on Hotel Riviers's beach
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.full-monte.com" rel="nofollow">
        Camp Full Monte
       </a>
       , A clothing optional, off-grid, eco campsite close the Montenegro/Croatia border crossing, run by an English couple.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Netherlands">
       Netherlands
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Netherlands">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Sauna_in_the_Dutch_language_area" title="Sauna in the Dutch language area">
       Public saunas
      </a>
      in the Netherlands are always mixed gender and nudity is the norm when using these. In the Netherlands tanning top free is legal on almost all beaches. Municipalities with a beach (usually including quiet parts) tend to have a nudist beach; even if the municipality does not like it, it designates a quiet part as such in order to be able to forbid nudity on the rest of the beach.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2009)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Almere" title="Almere">
        Almere
       </a>
       , Zilverstrand
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Amsterdamse_Bos" title="Amsterdamse Bos">
        Amsterdam, Amsterdamse Bos
       </a>
       , Zonneweide (from April 1 through September 30)
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">
        Amsterdam
       </a>
       a small beach near the lake Gasperplas (Metro station:Gasperplas).
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Bussloo" title="Bussloo">
        Bussloo
       </a>
       , longest nude beach in the Netherlands
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Bloemendaal_aan_Zee" title="Bloemendaal aan Zee">
        Bloemendaal aan Zee
       </a>
       , nude beach at the north part of the beach
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Zijpe" title="Zijpe">
        Callantsoog
       </a>
       , sandy beach 1.5km to the south - the oldest official nude beach in the country, dating from 1973
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Delft#Recreation" title="Delft">
        Delft, Grote Plas
       </a>
       , northeast side
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Scheveningen" title="Scheveningen">
        Scheveningen, The Hague
       </a>
       , sandy beach 1km to the north
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/The_Hague" title="The Hague">
        The Hague
       </a>
       , Zuiderstrand, approx. 300 m of sandy beach
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Kijkduin" title="Kijkduin">
        Kijkduin
       </a>
       , The Hague, 2 beaches
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/IJmuiden" title="IJmuiden">
        IJmuiden
       </a>
       , nude beach at the south part of the beach
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Zandvoort" title="Zandvoort">
        Zandvoort
       </a>
       , sandy beach 2km to the south
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Zeeland,_Stormvloedkering&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Zeeland, Stormvloedkering (page does not exist)">
        Zeeland, Stormvloedkering
       </a>
       , sandy beach 2km to the south
      </li>
     </ul>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Romania">
       Romania
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Romania">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Nudist beaches at
      <a href="/wiki/Neptun,_Romania" title="Neptun, Romania">
       Neptun
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Costine%C5%9Fti" title="Costineti">
       Costineti
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/2_Mai" title="2 Mai">
       2 Mai
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Vama_Veche" title="Vama Veche">
       Vama Veche
      </a>
      sea resorts, and the beach between
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eforie_Nord" title="Eforie Nord">
       Eforie Nord
      </a>
      and
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eforie_Sud" title="Eforie Sud">
       Eforie Sud
      </a>
      on the
      <a href="/wiki/Black_Sea" title="Black Sea">
       Black Sea
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      Topfree is tolerated on all beaches
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (July 2009)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
      .
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Russia">
       Russia
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Russia">
        edit
       </a>

        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       The Dunes Beach near
       <a href="/wiki/Sestroretsk" title="Sestroretsk">
        Sestroretsk
       </a>
       (north of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Petersburg" title="St. Petersburg">
        St. Petersburg
       </a>
       )
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-386">
        <a href="#cite_note-386">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         386
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       Divnomorskoe
      </li>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Spain">
       Spain
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Spain">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      Public nudity on the beach is not illegal in Spain. For nudity lovers, Spain offers various options for nude sunbathing. In addition to the long sandy beaches in the vicinity of large cities, topless sunbathing is possible on beaches in front of smaller villages. Hidden from view, nude sunbathing is always nice between the rocks of little coves besides the urbanisations.
     </p>
     <p>
      The various options can you see in the following pictures:
     </p>

       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mar_Bella_(beach)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mar Bella (beach) (page does not exist)">
        Mar Bella
       </a>
       beach is the primary clothing optional beach for the city of Barcelona.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Praia_de_Figueiras&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Praia de Figueiras (page does not exist)">
        Praia de Figueiras
       </a>
       also known as "Praia dos Alemns" on the
       <a href="/wiki/C%C3%ADes_Islands" title="Ces Islands">
        Ces Islands
       </a>
       in
       <a href="/wiki/Galicia_(Spain)" title="Galicia (Spain)">
        Galicia
       </a>
       .
      </li>
     </ul>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Sweden">
       Sweden
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>

       </a>

        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       Stockholm area:
       <ul>
        <li>
         gesta Nude Beach: Official nude beach on
         <a href="/wiki/Magelungen" title="Magelungen">
          Magelungen
         </a>
         , maintained by NF EOS, the Scandinavian Naturalist Federation. Located about 10km south of central Stockholm (
         <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion">
          <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;params=59_13_37_N_18_05_52_E_region:UA_scale:10000">
           <span class="geo-default">
            <span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">
             <span class="latitude">
              591337N
             </span>
             <span class="longitude">
              180552E
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="geo-multi-punct">
             / 
           </span>
           <span class="geo-nondefault">
            <span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">
             59.22694N 18.09778E
            </span>
            <span style="display:none">
              /
             <span class="geo">
              59.22694; 18.09778
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         ).
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-391">
          <a href="#cite_note-391">
           <span>
            [
           </span>
           391
           <span>
            ]
           </span>
          </a>
         </sup>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/L%C3%A5ngholmen" title="Lngholmen">
          Lngholmen
         </a>
         : Unofficial ("spontaneous") nude beach, located on the western end of Lngholmen island (
         <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion">
          <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;params=59_19_17_N_18_00_56_E_region:UA_scale:10000">
           <span class="geo-default">
            <span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">
             <span class="latitude">
              591917N
             </span>
             <span class="longitude">
              180056E
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="geo-multi-punct">
             / 
           </span>
           <span class="geo-nondefault">
            <span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">

           </span>
          </a>

        </li>
        <li>
         Klltorp Nude Beach: Unofficial ("spontaneous") nude beach, located about 6km southeast of central Stockholm, on the southeastern end of Klltorp lake (
         <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion">

        </li>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Switzerland">
       Switzerland
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Switzerland">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      While there are no official nudist areas, going topfree is accepted in all parts of the country, including central
      <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">
       Geneva
      </a>
      . Saturdays and Sundays in
      <a href="/wiki/Lausanne" title="Lausanne">
       Lausanne
      </a>
      are unofficial nudist days, and discounts are often offered in shops to the first nude customer of the day.
      <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
       [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
         <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2015)">
          citation needed
         </span>
        </a>
       </i>
       ]
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Turkey">
       Turkey
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Turkey">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Patara_Beach" title="Patara Beach">
        Patara Beach
       </a>
       . This is the longest sandy beach in Turkey and one of the largest in the whole Mediterranean. More than 20km of sand where many people go completely naked after certain distance to the public. Naked people also socialize with each other too. Local police and gendarme know about the status and no problem with nudity.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Bodrum_Haremtan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Bodrum Haremtan (page does not exist)">
        Bodrum Haremtan
       </a>
       . This is actually a rocky wild shore where mostly gays go there to socialize naked. Since the shore is very visible from the Bodrum port entry, it seems many of the locals know about the place. It is also very old and have been visited for more than 15 years.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Altinkum_Cesme&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Altinkum Cesme (page does not exist)">
        Altinkum Cesme
       </a>
       . This is a very nice nude beach where many people of every orientation visit. You can see locals, tourists, men, women fully naked in Summer. Beware of pickpockets and park your cars etc. in safe locations.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2012)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       (That seems a bit odd, to "beware of Pickpockets" at a nude beach)
      </li>
     </ul>

       </a>
       , between
       <a href="/wiki/Barmouth" title="Barmouth">
        Barmouth
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Harlech" title="Harlech">
        Harlech
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Gwynedd" title="Gwynedd">
        Gwynedd
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Tything_Barn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Tything Barn (page does not exist)">
        Tything Barn
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Pembrokeshire" title="Pembrokeshire">
        Pembrokeshire
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/West_Wales" title="West Wales">
        West Wales
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Scotland">
       Scotland
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_social_nudity_places_in_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Scotland">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Cleat%27s_Shore&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cleat's Shore (page does not exist)">
        Cleat's Shore
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Isle_of_Arran" title="Isle of Arran">
        Isle of Arran
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Firth_of_Clyde" title="Firth of Clyde">
        Firth of Clyde
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Ardeer,_Scotland" title="Ardeer, Scotland">

       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/North_Ayrshire" title="North Ayrshire">
        North Ayrshire
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Firth_of_Clyde" title="Firth of Clyde">
        Firth of Clyde
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Toplessness" title="Toplessness">
        Topless
       </a>
       tolerated on most beaches.
      </li>
